2026-04-20 11:35:31.150 +05:30 [INF] Executed DbCommand (15ms) [Parameters=[@__customerId_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [t].[CustomerID], [t].[FullName], [t].[Email], [t0].[PolicyID], [t0].[PlanName], [t0].[SchemeName], [t0].[PolicyDetails], [t0].[Premium], [t0].[DateIssued], [t0].[MaturityPeriod], [t0].[PolicyLapseDate], [t0].[SchemeID], [t0].[PlanID], [t0].[PaymentID], [t0].[Amount], [t0].[PaymentDate]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [c].[CustomerID], [c].[FullName], [c].[Email]
    FROM [Customer] AS [c]
    WHERE [c].[CustomerID] = @__customerId_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[PolicyID], [i].[PlanName], [s].[SchemeName], [p].[PolicyDetails], [p].[Premium], [p].[DateIssued], [p].[MaturityPeriod], [p].[PolicyLapseDate], [s].[SchemeID], [i].[PlanID], [p0].[PaymentID], [p0].[Amount], [p0].[PaymentDate], [p].[CustomerID]
    FROM [Policy] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [Scheme] AS [s] ON [p].[SchemeID] = [s].[SchemeID]
    INNER JOIN [InsurancePlan] AS [i] ON [s].[PlanID] = [i].[PlanID]
    LEFT JOIN [Payment] AS [p0] ON [p].[PolicyID] = [p0].[PolicyID]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[CustomerID] = [t0].[CustomerID]
